	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'ec26e007b0f1290828d7c41e89fec63f07b36749') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ec26e007b0f1290828d7c41e89fec63f07b36749') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c013f37c6de39d29ef7125fb0709aa0987cd9750') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ec26e007b0f1290828d7c41e89fec63f07b36749') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '685c35930317c6f7e64b4da8df7cedfc8a4b2436') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '685c35930317c6f7e64b4da8df7cedfc8a4b2436') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '012c9276d782ee73d95669477de2b71ab3590013') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '685c35930317c6f7e64b4da8df7cedfc8a4b2436') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') != '2ca8a875ab4ba59382699f3d73f46167c3e2686b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '2ca8a875ab4ba59382699f3d73f46167c3e2686b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '6e3963b0b3ffc910241852ee2aeab67fd9a1a83d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '2ca8a875ab4ba59382699f3d73f46167c3e2686b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_45();
	if (!is_file('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php') != '68856b65f651666de935e86eb9c894ce19e0b0b5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php') !== '68856b65f651666de935e86eb9c894ce19e0b0b5') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php') !== '0886b3a82d1155475272d6782bd54a63c0400805') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_45();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php') !== '68856b65f651666de935e86eb9c894ce19e0b0b5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/200_log/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}
